Here's the complete solution:\n\n## Implementation Summary\n\n### What Was Changed\nModified `/workspace/extensions/typescript-language-features/src/languageFeatures/diagnostics.ts` to add file system change listeners in the `DiagnosticsManager` constructor.\n\n### The Fix Explained\n\n**Before:** The diagnostics system only responded to `onDidChangeTextDocument` events (user edits in the editor). When files changed on disk (Git branch switches), the stale diagnostics were never cleared.\n\n**After:** A file system watcher monitors all TypeScript/JavaScript files. When files change or are deleted on disk:\n1. The file watcher detects the change\n2. We call `deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile()` to clear cached diagnostics  \n3. The TypeScript server re-analyzes the file\n4.
